<a name="fm-AreaRegionService"></a>

### AreaRegionService


| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| CreateArea | [CreateAreaRequest](#fm-CreateAreaRequest) | [UpsertAreaResponse](#fm-UpsertAreaResponse) | Create a new Area. Authorization scope of `fm.area.create` is required |
| ListArea | [ListAreaRequest](#fm-ListAreaRequest) | [ListAreaResponse](#fm-ListAreaResponse) | List returns the list of Area ascending order of Area title |
| UpdateArea | [UpdateAreaRequest](#fm-UpdateAreaRequest) | [UpsertAreaResponse](#fm-UpsertAreaResponse) | Update existing Area. Authorization scope of `fm.area.update` is required |
| DeleteArea | [DeleteAreaRequest](#fm-DeleteAreaRequest) | [DeleteAreaResponse](#fm-DeleteAreaResponse) | Delete existing Area. Authorization scope of `fm.area.delete` is required |
| CreateSubArea | [CreateSubAreaRequest](#fm-CreateSubAreaRequest) | [UpsertSubAreaResponse](#fm-UpsertSubAreaResponse) | Create a new Sub-Area. Authorization scope of `fm.sub-area.create` is required |
| UpdateSubArea | [UpdateSubAreaRequest](#fm-UpdateSubAreaRequest) | [UpsertSubAreaResponse](#fm-UpsertSubAreaResponse) | Update existing Sub Area. Authorization scope of `fm.sub-area.update` is required |
| DeleteSubArea | [DeleteSubAreaRequest](#fm-DeleteSubAreaRequest) | [DeleteSubAreaResponse](#fm-DeleteSubAreaResponse) | Delete existing Sub-Area of an Area. Authorizaton scope of `fm.sub-area.delete` is required |
| CreateRegion | [CreateRegionRequest](#fm-CreateRegionRequest) | [UpsertRegionResponse](#fm-UpsertRegionResponse) | Create a new Region. Authorization scope of `fm.region.create` is required |
| ListRegion | [ListRegionRequest](#fm-ListRegionRequest) | [ListRegionResponse](#fm-ListRegionResponse) | List returns the list of regions ascending order of region title |
| UpdateRegion | [UpdateRegionRequest](#fm-UpdateRegionRequest) | [UpsertRegionResponse](#fm-UpsertRegionResponse) | Create a new Region. Authorization scope of `fm.region.update` is required |
| DeleteRegion | [DeleteRegionRequest](#fm-DeleteRegionRequest) | [DeleteRegionResponse](#fm-DeleteRegionResponse) | Delete an existing Region. Authorization scope of `fm.region.delete` is required |

 



<a name="check_service-proto"></a>
<p align="right"><a href="#top">Top</a></p>

## check_service.proto



<a name="fm-CheckInOutRequest"></a>

### CheckInOutRequest
Request for checking in to opening_check and checking out to closing_check


| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| check_id | [string](#string) |  | check in or out to particular check item with check_id |






<a name="fm-CreateCheckRequest"></a>

### CreateCheckRequest
Request to create check


| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| title | [string](#string) |  | title of the check |
| instruction | [string](#string) |  | detail instruction of the opening_check |
| employee_id | [string](#string) |  | employee the opening_check is assigned to |
| check_type | [string](#string) |  | check_type = opening for opening check and check_type = closing for closing check |
| start_time | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | check must start by at least this time. Start time is combination of appointment date and time |
| organization_id | [string](#string) |  | organization id |






<a name="fm-CreateCheckResponse"></a>

### CreateCheckResponse
Response from create check


| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| check_id | [string](#string) |  | unique id of the check |






<a name="fm-CreateEmployeeCheckRequest"></a>

### CreateEmployeeCheckRequest



| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| employee_id | [string](#string) |  | id of employee who is about to check in or check out |
| organization_id | [string](#string) |  | organization id of the employee |
| check_type | [string](#string) |  | type of check i.e. check in or check out |
| reason | [string](#string) |  | reason |
| checked_details | [string](#string) | repeated | checked details ids |






<a name="fm-CreateEmployeeCheckResponse"></a>

### CreateEmployeeCheckResponse



| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| employee_check_id | [string](#string) |  | employee check id |






<a name="fm-CreateOpeningClosingCheckRequest"></a>

### CreateOpeningClosingCheckRequest



| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| check_type | [string](#string) |  | check whether it is a check_in or check_out |
| organization_id | [string](#string) |  | organization id |
| type | [string](#string) |  | type of opening/closing: GLOBAL, EMPLOYEE, GROUP |
| employee_id | [string](#string) |  | unique id of employee (optional / required for type=EMPLOYEE) |
| employee_ids | [string](#string) | repeated | list of employees (optional / required for type=GROUP) |
| client_ids | [string](#string) | repeated | unique id of clients (optional) |
| designation_ids | [string](#string) | repeated | unique id of designations (optional) |
| department_id | [string](#string) |  | unique id of department (optional) |
| designation_id | [string](#string) |  | unique id of designation (optional) |
| display_date | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | Date on which opening/closing check is shown (required if is_recurrence is false) |
| details | [string](#string) | repeated | List of instructions |
| is_recurrence | [bool](#bool) |  | wether opening/closing check is recurrence |
| recurrence | [UpsertRecurrence](#fm-UpsertRecurrence) |  | details of recurrence |






<a name="fm-CreateOpeningClosingCheckResponse"></a>

### CreateOpeningClosingCheckResponse



| Field | Type | Label | Description |

<a name="fm-ListCheckResponse-CheckResponse"></a>

### ListCheckResponse.CheckResponse
Check definition


| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| check_id | [string](#string) |  | unique identifier for the check |
| title | [string](#string) |  | title of the check |
| instruction | [string](#string) |  | detail instruction of the check |
| employee_id | [string](#string) |  | employee the check is assigned to |
| start_time | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | check must start by at least this time. Start time is combination of appointment date and time |
| check_time | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | checked in time for check_type=opening or checked out time for check_type=closing |
| check_type | [string](#string) |  | check_type = opening for opening check and check_type = closing for closing check |
| created_at | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | time generated by system at the instance the opening_check was created |
| organization_id | [string](#string) |  | organization id of the check |

<a name="fm-CheckService"></a>

### CheckService
service to manage check list which should be checked before starting task and
checked after task

| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| Create | [CreateCheckRequest](#fm-CreateCheckRequest) | [CreateCheckResponse](#fm-CreateCheckResponse) | Create a new check. Authorization scope of `fm.check.create` is required. |
| CheckInOut | [CheckInOutRequest](#fm-CheckInOutRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Check can be used to check in a staff to a opening_check and check out to a closing check Authorization scope of `fm.check.in` and `fm.check.out` is required. |
| List | [ListCheckRequest](#fm-ListCheckRequest) | [ListCheckResponse](#fm-ListCheckResponse) | List returns the list of check visible to the authroized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.check.list` is required. |
| CreateOpeningClosingCheck | [CreateOpeningClosingCheckRequest](#fm-CreateOpeningClosingCheckRequest) | [CreateOpeningClosingCheckResponse](#fm-CreateOpeningClosingCheckResponse) | Add opening/closing check. Authorization scope of `fm.global-check.update` is required |
| UpdateOpeningClosingCheck | [UpdateOpeningClosingCheckRequest](#fm-UpdateOpeningClosingCheckRequest) | [UpdateOpeningClosingCheckResponse](#fm-UpdateOpeningClosingCheckResponse) | Edit opening/closing check. Authorization scope of `fm.global-check.update` is required |
| DeleteOpeningClosingCheck | [DeleteOpeningClosingCheckRequest](#fm-DeleteOpeningClosingCheckRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Delete opening/closing check. Authorization scope of `fm.global-check.update` is required |
| ListOpeningClosingCheck | [ListOpeningClosingCheckRequest](#fm-ListOpeningClosingCheckRequest) | [ListOpeningClosingCheckResponse](#fm-ListOpeningClosingCheckResponse) | List opening/closing check. Authorization scope of `fm.global-check.update` is required |
| ListGlobalCheck | [ListGlobalCheckRequest](#fm-ListGlobalCheckRequest) | [ListGlobalCheckResponse](#fm-ListGlobalCheckResponse) | ListGlobalCheck returns the list of global checks visible to the authorized user in descending order of created date. Authorization scope of `fm.global-check.list` is required. |
| UpsertGlobalDescription | [UpsertGlobalDescriptionRequest](#fm-UpsertGlobalDescriptionRequest) | [UpsertGlobalDescriptionResponse](#fm-UpsertGlobalDescriptionResponse) | UpsertGlobalDescription creates and updates the description for opening/closing check Authorization scope of `fm.global-check.update` is required |
| GetGlobalDescription | [GetGlobalDescriptionRequest](#fm-GetGlobalDescriptionRequest) | [GetGlobalDescriptionResponse](#fm-GetGlobalDescriptionResponse) | GetGlobalDescription returns the details of global description on the basis of check type Authorization scope of `fm.global-check.list` is required. |
| CreateEmployeeCheck | [CreateEmployeeCheckRequest](#fm-CreateEmployeeCheckRequest) | [CreateEmployeeCheckResponse](#fm-CreateEmployeeCheckResponse) | Create employee check. Authorization scope of `fm.employee-check.create` is required |
| GetEmployeeCheck | [GetEmployeeCheckRequest](#fm-GetEmployeeCheckRequest) | [GetEmployeeCheckResponse](#fm-GetEmployeeCheckResponse) | Get individual employee checks information. Authorization scope of `fm.employee-check.detail` is required |
| ListEmployeeCheck | [ListEmployeeCheckRequest](#fm-ListEmployeeCheckRequest) | [ListEmployeeCheckResponse](#fm-ListEmployeeCheckResponse) | Get checks information of multiple employees. Authorization scope of `fm.employee-check.list` is required |

<a name="fm-GetTargetTasksRequest"></a>

### GetTargetTasksRequest

<a name="fm-ClientEmployeeService"></a>

### ClientEmployeeService


| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| Create | [CreateClientEmployeeRequest](#fm-CreateClientEmployeeRequest) | [CreateClientEmployeeResponse](#fm-CreateClientEmployeeResponse) | Create a new client employee relation(many to many). this helps to assign employee to the client. Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.create` is required. |
| List | [ListClientEmployeeRequest](#fm-ListClientEmployeeRequest) | [ListClientEmployeeResponse](#fm-ListClientEmployeeResponse) | List the employees assigned in the clients Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.list` is required. |
| AssignShift | [AssignClientEmployeeShiftRequest](#fm-AssignClientEmployeeShiftRequest) | [AssignClientEmployeeShiftResponse](#fm-AssignClientEmployeeShiftResponse) | Assign shift to the employee for the client Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.assign-shift` is required. |
| AssignContractedHours | [AssignContractedHoursRequest](#fm-AssignContractedHoursRequest) | [AssignContractedHoursResponse](#fm-AssignContractedHoursResponse) | Assign contracted hours to the employee for the client Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.assign-contracted-hours` is required. |
| GetContractedHours | [GetContractedHoursRequest](#fm-GetContractedHoursRequest) | [GetContractedHoursResponse](#fm-GetContractedHoursResponse) | Get contracted hours of the employee for the client Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.get-contracted-hours` is required. |
| GetContractedHoursByClient | [GetContractedHoursByClientRequest](#fm-GetContractedHoursByClientRequest) | [GetContractedHoursByClientResponse](#fm-GetContractedHoursByClientResponse) | Get contracted hours of the multiple employees of a signle client(by id) Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.get-contracted-hours-by-client` is required. |
| GetContractedHoursByEmployee | [GetContractedHoursByEmployeeRequest](#fm-GetContractedHoursByEmployeeRequest) | [GetContractedHoursByEmployeeResponse](#fm-GetContractedHoursByEmployeeResponse) | Get contracted hours of a employees for his/her multiplr clients Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.get-contracted-hours-by-employee` is required. |
| AssignTargetTasks | [AssignTargetTasksRequest](#fm-AssignTargetTasksRequest) | [AssignTargetTasksResponse](#fm-AssignTargetTasksResponse) | Assign target tasks for each day of the week in a fixed interval of time for an employee for a client Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.assign-target-tasks` is required. |
| GetTargetTasks | [GetTargetTasksRequest](#fm-GetTargetTasksRequest) | [GetTargetTasksResponse](#fm-GetTargetTasksResponse) | Get the assigned target tasks of an employee for a client Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.get-target-tasks` is required. |
| GetClientEmployeeIdsByEmployeeId | [GetClientEmployeeIdsByEmployeeRequest](#fm-GetClientEmployeeIdsByEmployeeRequest) | [GetClientEmployeeIdsByEmployeeResponse](#fm-GetClientEmployeeIdsByEmployeeResponse) | Get client_employee_ids by employee_id Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.get-client-employee-ids-by-employee-id` is required. |
| GetClientIdsByEmployeeId | [GetClientIdsByEmployeeRequest](#fm-GetClientIdsByEmployeeRequest) | [GetClientIdsByEmployeeResponse](#fm-GetClientIdsByEmployeeResponse) | Get client_ids by employee_id Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.get-client-ids-by-employee-id` is required. |
| GetEmployeeIdsByClientId | [GetEmployeeIdsByClientIdRequest](#fm-GetEmployeeIdsByClientIdRequest) | [GetEmployeeIdsByClientIdResponse](#fm-GetEmployeeIdsByClientIdResponse) | Get employees by Client_id Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.get-employee-ids-by-client-id` is required. |
| CreateEmployeeTraining | [CreateEmployeeTrainingRequest](#fm-CreateEmployeeTrainingRequest) | [CreateEmployeeTrainingResponse](#fm-CreateEmployeeTrainingResponse) | Create training for employee of client Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.create-employee-training` is required |
| GetEmployeeTraining | [GetEmployeeTrainingRequest](#fm-GetEmployeeTrainingRequest) | [GetEmployeeTrainingResponse](#fm-GetEmployeeTrainingResponse) | Get employee trainings Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.get-employee-trainings` is required. |
| CreateTransfer | [CreateTransferRequest](#fm-CreateTransferRequest) | [CreateTransferResponse](#fm-CreateTransferResponse) | Create a new transfer. Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.transfer.create` is required. |
| ListTransfer | [ListTransferRequest](#fm-ListTransferRequest) | [ListTransferResponse](#fm-ListTransferResponse) | List transfers. Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.transfer.list` is required. |
| CreateFeedback | [CreateFeedbackRequest](#fm-CreateFeedbackRequest) | [CreateFeedbackResponse](#fm-CreateFeedbackResponse) | Create a new feedback. Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.feedback.create` is required. |
| ListFeedback | [ListFeedbackRequest](#fm-ListFeedbackRequest) | [ListFeedbackResponse](#fm-ListFeedbackResponse) | List feedbacks. Authorization scope of `fm.client-employee.feedback.list` is required. |

### ClientService


| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| Create | [CreateClientRequest](#fm-CreateClientRequest) | [CreateClientResponse](#fm-CreateClientResponse) | Create a new client. Authorization scope of `fm.client.create` is required. |
| List | [ListClientRequest](#fm-ListClientRequest) | [ListClientResponse](#fm-ListClientResponse) | List returns the list of client visible to the authorized user in descending order. Scope of `fm.client.list` is required. |
| Update | [UpdateClientRequest](#fm-UpdateClientRequest) | [UpdateClientResponse](#fm-UpdateClientResponse) | Update an existing client. Authorization scope of `fm.client.update` is required. |
| CreateLead | [CreateClientRequest](#fm-CreateClientRequest) | [CreateClientResponse](#fm-CreateClientResponse) | Create a new client lead Authorization scope of `fm.client.lead` is required. |
| LeadStatusChange | [LeadStatusChangeRequest](#fm-LeadStatusChangeRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Change lead client status Authorization scope of `fm.client.lead` is required. |
| TransferLeadToProspect | [TransferLeadToProspectRequest](#fm-TransferLeadToProspectRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Transfer lead to prospect Authorization scope of `fm.cleint.prospect` is required. |
| UpdateClientArea | [UpdateClientAreaRequest](#fm-UpdateClientAreaRequest) | [UpdateClientAreaResponse](#fm-UpdateClientAreaResponse) | Update area of clients if it is empty. Authorization scope of `fm.client.update` is required. |
| DeleteClientArea | [DeleteClientAreaRequest](#fm-DeleteClientAreaRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Make area field null. Authorization scope of `fm.client.update` is required. |
| UpdateClientRegion | [UpdateClientRegionRequest](#fm-UpdateClientRegionRequest) | [UpdateClientRegionResponse](#fm-UpdateClientRegionResponse) | Update region of clients if it is empty. Authorization scope of `fm.client.update` is required. |
| DeleteClientRegion | [DeleteClientRegionRequest](#fm-DeleteClientRegionRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Make region field null. Authorization scope of `fm.client.update` is required. |
| Detail | [ClientDetailRequest](#fm-ClientDetailRequest) | [ClientDetailResponse](#fm-ClientDetailResponse) | Details of client. Scope of `fm.client.detail` is required. |
| ClientConfidentialDetail | [ClientConfidentialDetailRequest](#fm-ClientConfidentialDetailRequest) | [ClientConfidentialDetailResponse](#fm-ClientConfidentialDetailResponse) | Returns confidential details of a client. Authorization scope of `fm.client.confidential` is required. |
| UpdateClientConfidential | [UpdateClientConfidentialRequest](#fm-UpdateClientConfidentialRequest) | [UpdateClientConfidentialResponse](#fm-UpdateClientConfidentialResponse) | Updates the confidential details of a client. Authorization scope of `fm.client.confidential` is required. |
| DateDetail | [ClientDateDetailRequest](#fm-ClientDateDetailRequest) | [ClientDateDetailResponse](#fm-ClientDateDetailResponse) | Client Date Details scope of `fm.client.list` is required. |
| ChangeStatus | [ClientChangeStatusRequest](#fm-ClientChangeStatusRequest) | [ClientChangeStatusResponse](#fm-ClientChangeStatusResponse) | Change status of a client. Scope of `fm.client.status-change` is required. |

| ListAttachment | [ClientListAttachmentRequest](#fm-ClientListAttachmentRequest) | [ClientListAttachmentResponse](#fm-ClientListAttachmentResponse) | Lists attachment for a client. Scope of `fm.client.list-attachment` is required. |

<a name="fm-DepartmentService"></a>

### DepartmentService


| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| Create | [CreateDepartmentRequest](#fm-CreateDepartmentRequest) | [CreateDepartmentResponse](#fm-CreateDepartmentResponse) | Create a new department. Authorization scope of `fm.department.create` is required |
| List | [ListDepartmentRequest](#fm-ListDepartmentRequest) | [ListDepartmentResponse](#fm-ListDepartmentResponse) | List returns the list of department visible to the authroized user in ascending order of department title |
| Update | [UpdateDepartmentRequest](#fm-UpdateDepartmentRequest) | [UpdateDepartmentResponse](#fm-UpdateDepartmentResponse) | Update department of an organization. Authorization scope of `fm.department.update` is required |
| Delete | [DeleteDepartmentRequest](#fm-DeleteDepartmentRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Delete a department. Authorization scope of `fm.department.delete` is required |
| CreateTrainingType | [CreateTrainingTypeRequest](#fm-CreateTrainingTypeRequest) | [CreateTrainingTypeResponse](#fm-CreateTrainingTypeResponse) | Create a new training type Authorization scope of `fm.training-type.create` is required |
| ListTrainingType | [ListTrainingTypeRequest](#fm-ListTrainingTypeRequest) | [ListTrainingTypeResponse](#fm-ListTrainingTypeResponse) | ListTrainingType returns the list of training type visible to the authorized user in ascending order of training type title |
| UpdateTrainingType | [UpdateTrainingTypeRequest](#fm-UpdateTrainingTypeRequest) | [UpdateTrainingTypeResponse](#fm-UpdateTrainingTypeResponse) | Update training type. Authorization scope of `fm.training-type.update` is required |
| DeleteTrainingType | [DeleteTrainingTypeRequest](#fm-DeleteTrainingTypeRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Delete a training type. Authorization scope of `fm.training-type.delete` is required |

<a name="fm-EmployeeService"></a>

### EmployeeService


| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| Create | [CreateEmployeeRequest](#fm-CreateEmployeeRequest) | [CreateEmployeeResponse](#fm-CreateEmployeeResponse) | Create a new employee. Authorization scope of `fm.employee.create` is required. |
| List | [ListEmployeeRequest](#fm-ListEmployeeRequest) | [ListEmployeeResponse](#fm-ListEmployeeResponse) | List returns the list of employee visible to the authroized user in descending order. Authorization scope of `fm.employee.list` is required. |
| Update | [UpdateEmployeeRequest](#fm-UpdateEmployeeRequest) | [UpdateEmployeeResponse](#fm-UpdateEmployeeResponse) | Update an existing employee. Authorization scope of `fm.employee.update` is required. |
| Detail | [EmployeeDetailRequest](#fm-EmployeeDetailRequest) | [EmployeeDetailResponse](#fm-EmployeeDetailResponse) | Details of employee. Scope of `fm.employee.detail` is required. |
| ConfidentialDetail | [EmployeeConfidentialDetailRequest](#fm-EmployeeConfidentialDetailRequest) | [EmployeeConfidentialDetailResponse](#fm-EmployeeConfidentialDetailResponse) | Returns confidential details of an employee. Authorization scope of `fm.employee.confidential` is required. |
| UpdateEmployeeConfidential | [UpdateEmployeeConfidentialRequest](#fm-UpdateEmployeeConfidentialRequest) | [UpdateEmployeeConfidentialResponse](#fm-UpdateEmployeeConfidentialResponse) | Updates the confidential details of an employee. Authorization scope of `fm.employee.confidential` is required. |
| UpdateStatus | [UpdateEmployeeStatusRequest](#fm-UpdateEmployeeStatusRequest) | [UpdateEmployeeStatusResponse](#fm-UpdateEmployeeStatusResponse) | Update an employee status Authorization scope of `fm.employee.update-status` is required. |
| AddAttachment | [EmployeeAddAttachmentRequest](#fm-EmployeeAddAttachmentRequest) | [EmployeeAddAttachmentResponse](#fm-EmployeeAddAttachmentResponse) | Adds attachment for an employee. Scope of `fm.employee.add-attachment` is required. |
| ListAttachment | [EmployeeListAttachmentRequest](#fm-EmployeeListAttachmentRequest) | [EmployeeListAttachmentResponse](#fm-EmployeeListAttachmentResponse) | Lists attachment for an employee. Scope of `fm.employee.list-attachment` is required. |
| DeleteAttachment | [EmployeeDeleteAttachmentRequest](#fm-EmployeeDeleteAttachmentRequest) | [EmployeeDeleteAttachmentResponse](#fm-EmployeeDeleteAttachmentResponse) | Soft deletes an attachment for an employee. Scope of `fm.employee.delete-attachment` is required. |

<a name="fm-InventoryService"></a>

### InventoryService
service to manage inventory available in an organization

| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| CreateInventoryItem | [CreateInventoryItemRequest](#fm-CreateInventoryItemRequest) | [CreateInventoryItemResponse](#fm-CreateInventoryItemResponse) | Create a new inventory item. Authorization scope of `fm.inventory.create` is required. |
| ListInventoryItem | [ListInventoryItemRequest](#fm-ListInventoryItemRequest) | [ListInventoryItemResponse](#fm-ListInventoryItemResponse) | Returns the list of inventory items in ascending order of name. Authorization scope of `fm.inventory.list` is required. |
| CreateInventoryCategory | [CreateInventoryCategoryRequest](#fm-CreateInventoryCategoryRequest) | [CreateInventoryCategoryResponse](#fm-CreateInventoryCategoryResponse) | Create a new inventory category. Authorization scope of `fm.inventory.category.create` is required. |
| ListInventoryCategory | [ListInventoryCategoryRequest](#fm-ListInventoryCategoryRequest) | [ListInventoryCategoryResponse](#fm-ListInventoryCategoryResponse) | Returns the list of inventory item categories in ascending order of name. Authorization scope of `fm.inventory.category.list` is required. |

<a name="fm-IssueService"></a>

### IssueService
service to manage issues

| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| CreateIssue | [CreateIssueRequest](#fm-CreateIssueRequest) | [CreateIssueResponse](#fm-CreateIssueResponse) | Create a new issue. Authorization scope of `fm.issue.create` is required. |
| ListIssues | [ListIssuesRequest](#fm-ListIssuesRequest) | [ListIssuesResponse](#fm-ListIssuesResponse) | List returns the list of all issues visible to the authroized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.issue.list` is required. |
| UpdateIssue | [UpdateIssueRequest](#fm-UpdateIssueRequest) | [UpdateIssueResponse](#fm-UpdateIssueResponse) | Update an existing issue. Authorization scope of `fm.issue.update` is required. |
| UpdateIssueStatus | [UpdateIssueStatusRequest](#fm-UpdateIssueStatusRequest) | [UpdateIssueStatusResponse](#fm-UpdateIssueStatusResponse) | Updates the status of an issue. Authorization scope of `fm.issue.status-update` is required. |
| DeleteIssue | [DeleteIssueRequest](#fm-DeleteIssueRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Deletes an existing issue. Authorization scope of `fm.issue.delete` is required. |

| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |

| Create | [CreateJobTypeRequest](#fm-CreateJobTypeRequest) | [CreateJobTypeResponse](#fm-CreateJobTypeResponse) | Create a new job type. Authorization scope of `fm.job-type.create` is required |
| List | [ListJobTypeRequest](#fm-ListJobTypeRequest) | [ListJobTypeResponse](#fm-ListJobTypeResponse) | List returns the list of job type visible to the authorized user in ascending order of job type title |

<a name="fm-JWTTokenService"></a>

### JWTTokenService
Genereates jwt tokens

| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| Login | [LoginRequest](#fm-LoginRequest) | [LoginResponse](#fm-LoginResponse) | authenticates user and returns tokens |
| Refresh | [RefreshRequest](#fm-RefreshRequest) | [LoginResponse](#fm-LoginResponse) | refresh an existing token and return new tokens |
| Logout | [LogoutRequest](#fm-LogoutRequest) | [LogoutResponse](#fm-LogoutResponse) | logout the user and invalidate refresh token |


<a name="fm-UserService"></a>

### UserService


| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| Create | [CreateUserRequest](#fm-CreateUserRequest) | [CreateUserResponse](#fm-CreateUserResponse) | Create a new user. Authorization scope of `fm.user.create` is required. |
| CreateUserOnEmployeeCreate | [CreateUserOnEmployeeCreateRequest](#fm-CreateUserOnEmployeeCreateRequest) | [CreateUserOnEmployeeCreateResponse](#fm-CreateUserOnEmployeeCreateResponse) | create user with no password and email is sent with password link Authorization scope of `fm.user.associate` is required. |
| UpsertScope | [UpsertScopeRequest](#fm-UpsertScopeRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Insert or update a scope group. Authorization scope of `` is required. |
| AssociateWithEmployee | [AssociateWithEmployeeRequest](#fm-AssociateWithEmployeeRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | associates login with an employee record. Authorization scope of `fm.user.associate` is required. |
| UpdateEmployeeScope | [UpdateEmployeeScopeRequest](#fm-UpdateEmployeeScopeRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | update scopes of user Authorization scope of `` is required. |
| GetAvailableRoles | [GetAvailableRoleRequest](#fm-GetAvailableRoleRequest) | [RoleResponse](#fm-RoleResponse) | get roles Authorization scope of `` is required. |
| GetAvailableScopes | [GetAvailableScopeRequest](#fm-GetAvailableScopeRequest) | [ScopeResponse](#fm-ScopeResponse) | get all scopes Authorization scope of `` is required |
| UpsertRole | [UpsertRoleRequest](#fm-UpsertRoleRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | insert or update role scopes. Authorization scope of `fm.role.create` and &#34;fm.role.update&#34; is required. |
| GetUserListByEmployeeIds | [GetUserListRequest](#fm-GetUserListRequest) | [GetUserListResponse](#fm-GetUserListResponse) | get user list according to employee id for changing roles/scopes Authorization scope of `` is required |
| GetUserListFromRole | [GetUserListFromRoleRequest](#fm-GetUserListFromRoleRequest) | [GetUserListFromRoleResponse](#fm-GetUserListFromRoleResponse) | get list of users from role name |
| ResetPassword | [ResetPasswordRequest](#fm-ResetPasswordRequest) | [ResetPasswordResponse](#fm-ResetPasswordResponse) | update password using token from email |
| ForgotPassword | [ForgotPasswordRequest](#fm-ForgotPasswordRequest) | [ForgotPasswordResponse](#fm-ForgotPasswordResponse) | forgot password endpoint |
| ChangePassword | [ChangePasswordRequest](#fm-ChangePasswordRequest) | [ChangePasswordResponse](#fm-ChangePasswordResponse) | change password endpoint for logged in user to change their own password |

<a name="fm-CreateMeetingRequest"></a>

### CreateMeetingRequest
Meeting creation request


| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| organization_id | [string](#string) |  | id of the organization this meeting belongs to |
| meeting_date | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | date of the meeting |
| estimated_time | [google.protobuf.Duration](#google-protobuf-Duration) |  | estimated time of the meeting |
| department_id | [string](#string) |  | id of department of generated meeting |
| employees_info | [Employees](#fm-Employees) |  | ids of employees |
| attendee_ids | [string](#string) | repeated | ids of employees who attend the meetings |
| agendas | [Agenda](#fm-Agenda) | repeated | information of agenda of the meetong |
| client_id | [string](#string) |  | required if meeting is for client else it is optional |
| title | [string](#string) |  | title of the meeting |

<a name="fm-MeetingService"></a>

### MeetingService


| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| Create | [CreateMeetingRequest](#fm-CreateMeetingRequest) | [CreateMeetingResponse](#fm-CreateMeetingResponse) | Create a new meeting. Authorization scope of `fm.meeting.create` is required. |
| List | [ListMeetingRequest](#fm-ListMeetingRequest) | [ListMeetingResponse](#fm-ListMeetingResponse) | List returns the list of meeting visible to the authorized user in descending order. Scope of `fm.meeting.list` is required. |
| Detail | [DetailMeetingRequest](#fm-DetailMeetingRequest) | [DetailMeetingResponse](#fm-DetailMeetingResponse) | Detail returns the detail of meeting along with its agendas, views, decisions and objections Attendees/Creator of meeting can view the details. |
| Update | [UpdateMeetingRequest](#fm-UpdateMeetingRequest) | [UpdateMeetingResponse](#fm-UpdateMeetingResponse) | Update an existing meeting. Authorization scope of `fm.meeting.update` is required. |
| UpdateMeetingStatus | [UpdateMeetingStatusRequest](#fm-UpdateMeetingStatusRequest) | [UpdateMeetingStatusResponse](#fm-UpdateMeetingStatusResponse) | Update status of a meeting. Authorization scope of `fm.meeting-status.update` is required. |
| AddAttendees | [AddAttendeesRequest](#fm-AddAttendeesRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Add Attendees to existing meetings. Authorization scope of `fm.meeting.update` is required. |
| AddAgendaView | [AddAgendaViewRequest](#fm-AddAgendaViewRequest) | [UpsertAgendaViewResponse](#fm-UpsertAgendaViewResponse) | Add views to a given agenda in a meeting. |
| EditAgendaView | [EditAgendaViewRequest](#fm-EditAgendaViewRequest) | [UpsertAgendaViewResponse](#fm-UpsertAgendaViewResponse) | Edit views of a given agenda in a meeting. |
| DeleteAgendaView | [DeleteAgendaViewRequest](#fm-DeleteAgendaViewRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Delete views of a given agenda in a meeting. |
| AddAgendaViewReply | [AddAgendaViewReplyRequest](#fm-AddAgendaViewReplyRequest) | [AddAgendaViewReplyResponse](#fm-AddAgendaViewReplyResponse) | Add reply to a given agenda view. |
| AddAgendaDecision | [AddAgendaDecisionRequest](#fm-AddAgendaDecisionRequest) | [UpsertAgendaDecisionResponse](#fm-UpsertAgendaDecisionResponse) | Add decision of an agenda |
| UpdateAgendaDecision | [UpdateAgendaDecisionRequest](#fm-UpdateAgendaDecisionRequest) | [UpsertAgendaDecisionResponse](#fm-UpsertAgendaDecisionResponse) | Update decision of an agenda |
| AddAgendaDecisionObjection | [AddAgendaDecisionObjectionRequest](#fm-AddAgendaDecisionObjectionRequest) | [UpsertAgendaDecisionObjectionResponse](#fm-UpsertAgendaDecisionObjectionResponse) | Add objection of decision of agenda |
| AddAgendaDecisionSupport | [AddAgendaDecisionSupportRequest](#fm-AddAgendaDecisionSupportRequest) | [AddAgendaDecisionSupportResponse](#fm-AddAgendaDecisionSupportResponse) | Add support to a decision of agenda |
| DeleteAgendaDecisionObjection | [DeleteAgendaDecisionObjectionRequest](#fm-DeleteAgendaDecisionObjectionRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Delete objection made for decisions of an agenda |
| AgendaTimerUpdate | [AgendaTimerRequest](#fm-AgendaTimerRequest) | [AgendaTimerResponse](#fm-AgendaTimerResponse) | start/stop agenda of meeting |
| MeetingTimerUpdate | [MeetingTimerUpdateRequest](#fm-MeetingTimerUpdateRequest) | [MeetingTimerUpdateResponse](#fm-MeetingTimerUpdateResponse) | start/stop meeting |
| CreateCall | [CreateCallRequest](#fm-CreateCallRequest) | [CreateCallResponse](#fm-CreateCallResponse) | Create a Call Authorization scope of `fm.call.create` is required. |
| ListCall | [ListCallRequest](#fm-ListCallRequest) | [ListCallResponse](#fm-ListCallResponse) | Returns the list of call visible to the authorized user in descending order Authorization scope of `fm.call.list` is required |
| UpdateCall | [UpdateCallRequest](#fm-UpdateCallRequest) | [UpdateCallResponse](#fm-UpdateCallResponse) | Update a call Authorization scope of `fm.call.update` is required |
| DeleteCall | [DeleteCallRequest](#fm-DeleteCallRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Delete a call Authorization scope of `fm.call,delete` is required |
| ListAllCount | [ListAllCountRequest](#fm-ListAllCountRequest) | [ListAllCountResponse](#fm-ListAllCountResponse) | List the count of call, issue, note and email. |
| CreateEmail | [CreateEmailRequest](#fm-CreateEmailRequest) | [CreateEmailResponse](#fm-CreateEmailResponse) | Creates an email. Authorization scope of `fm.email.create` is required. |
| ListEmail | [ListEmailRequest](#fm-ListEmailRequest) | [ListEmailResponse](#fm-ListEmailResponse) | Returns the list of emails visible to the authorized user in descending order. Authorization scope of `fm.email.list` is required. |
| UpdateEmail | [UpdateEmailRequest](#fm-UpdateEmailRequest) | [UpdateEmailResponse](#fm-UpdateEmailResponse) | Updates an email. Authorization scope of `fm.email.update` is required. |
| DeleteEmail | [DeleteEmailRequest](#fm-DeleteEmailRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Deletes an email. Authorization scope of `fm.email.delete` is required. |
| CreateMarketingCampaign | [CreateMarketingCampaignRequest](#fm-CreateMarketingCampaignRequest) | [CreateMarketingCampaignResponse](#fm-CreateMarketingCampaignResponse) | Creates a marketing-campaign. Authorization scope of `fm.marketing-campaign.create` is required. |
| UpdateMarketingCampaign | [UpdateMarketingCampaignRequest](#fm-UpdateMarketingCampaignRequest) | [UpdateMarketingCampaignResponse](#fm-UpdateMarketingCampaignResponse) | Updates a marketing-campaign. Authorization scope of `fm.marketing-campaign.update` is required. |
| ListMarketingCampaign | [ListMarketingCampaignRequest](#fm-ListMarketingCampaignRequest) | [ListMarketingCampaignResponse](#fm-ListMarketingCampaignResponse) | Returns the list of campaigns visible to the authorized user in descending order. Authorization scope of `fm.marketing-campaign.list` is required. |
| DeleteMarketingCampaign | [DeleteMarketingCampaignRequest](#fm-DeleteMarketingCampaignRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Deletes an existing marketing-campaign. Authorization scope of `fm.marketing-campaign.delete` is required. |

<a name="fm-CreateTaskRequest"></a>

### CreateTaskRequest
Request to create task


| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| title | [string](#string) |  | title (name) of the task |
| description | [string](#string) |  | description of the task |
| client_id | [string](#string) |  | client the task is associated with. Optional |
| employee_id | [string](#string) |  | employee the task is assigned to |
| start_time | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | task must start by at least this time. Start time is combination of appointment date and time |
| estimate_time | [google.protobuf.Duration](#google-protobuf-Duration) |  | the estimated time period to complete the task |
| organization_id | [string](#string) |  | the organization of the employee |
| is_variation | [bool](#bool) |  | flag to confirm if the task is variation or not |
| is_vary | [bool](#bool) |  | whether task is vary or not |
| is_break | [bool](#bool) |  | if break is true or false |
| break_type | [string](#string) |  | if break is paid or unpaid |
| is_recurrence | [bool](#bool) |  | whether task is recurrence |
| task_type | [string](#string) |  | type of task: Allowed [&#34;DOC&#34;, &#34;VARIATION&#34;, &#34;MOBILE&#34;, &#34;OTHERS&#34;, &#34;PERIODIC(REGULAR)&#34;, &#34;PERIODIC(ONE OFF)&#34;, &#34;PERIODIC(WINDOW)&#34;, &#34;PERIODIC(ACCOMODATION)&#34;] |
| recurrence | [UpsertRecurrence](#fm-UpsertRecurrence) |  | details of recurrence |

| employee_id | [string](#string) |  | Employee id of the associated employee |
| client_id | [string](#string) |  | Client id |
| organization_id | [string](#string) |  | Organization id of the employee |
| type | [string](#string) |  | type of leave i.e. HOLIDAY, SICK OR ABSENT |
| payment_type | [string](#string) |  | type of payment i.e. PAID OR UNPAID |
| description | [string](#string) |  | description regarding the leave |
| approved_by | [string](#string) |  | id of emoloyee who approved |
| rejected_by | [string](#string) |  | id of employee who rejected |
| status | [string](#string) |  | status i.e. PENDING, APPROVED OR REJECTED |
| created_at | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | timestamp at which the employee absence was created |
| dates | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) | repeated | dates for which leave is taken |
| covers | [ListCoverData](#fm-ListCoverData) | repeated | All covers of absence |

<a name="fm-TaskResponse"></a>

### TaskResponse
Task definition


| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| task_id | [string](#string) |  | unique identifier for the task |
| title | [string](#string) |  | title (name) of the task |
| description | [string](#string) |  | description of the task |
| client_id | [string](#string) |  | client the task is associated with. Optional |
| employee_id | [string](#string) |  | employee the task is assigned to |
| start_time | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | task must start by at least this time. Start time is combination of appointment date and time |
| estimate_time | [google.protobuf.Duration](#google-protobuf-Duration) |  | the estimated time period to complete the task |
| actual_in | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | time the task was checked in |
| actual_out | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | time the task was checked out |
| created_at | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | time generated by system at the instance the task was created |
| organization_id | [string](#string) |  | organization id of the employee |
| is_variation | [bool](#bool) |  | flag to confirm if the task is variation or not |
| approved_correction | [google.protobuf.Duration](#google-protobuf-Duration) |  | approved correction duration of the task |
| is_vary | [bool](#bool) |  | flag to confirm if the task is vary or not |
| is_break | [bool](#bool) |  | to check break, true or false |
| break_type | [string](#string) |  | to check break type, paid or unpaid |
| task_type | [string](#string) |  | type of task: Allowed [&#34;DOC&#34;, &#34;VARIATION&#34;, &#34;MOBILE&#34;, &#34;OTHERS&#34;, &#34;PERIODIC(REGULAR)&#34;, &#34;PERIODIC(ONE OFF)&#34;, &#34;PERIODIC(WINDOW)&#34;, &#34;PERIODIC(ACCOMODATION)&#34;] |
| is_recurrence | [bool](#bool) |  | wether task is recurrence |
| recurrence | [RecurrenceDetails](#fm-RecurrenceDetails) |  | details of recurrence |
| recurrence_parent_task | [string](#string) |  | Id of task from which current task was generated |
| vary_time | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | Date/time at which vary task should be initiated |
| correction_data | [TaskResponse.TaskCorrectionData](#fm-TaskResponse-TaskCorrectionData) |  | Correction data regardless of status |
| employee_absence | [TaskResponse.TaskEmployeeAbsence](#fm-TaskResponse-TaskEmployeeAbsence) |  | Employee Absence Data |






<a name="fm-TaskResponse-TaskCorrectionData"></a>

### TaskResponse.TaskCorrectionData



| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| task_correction_id | [string](#string) |  | unique id of task correction |
| correction | [google.protobuf.Duration](#google-protobuf-Duration) |  | correction time of the task report |
| status | [string](#string) |  | status of the correction |
| corrected_by | [string](#string) |  | name of the person who correctes timesheet |
| approved_by | [string](#string) |  | name of the person who approves this correction |
| is_negative | [bool](#bool) |  | whether the correction time is negative or not |

<a name="fm-UpdateTaskRequest"></a>

### UpdateTaskRequest
Request to update task


| Field | Type | Label | Description |
| ----- | ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| task_id | [string](#string) |  | unique id of the task |

| description | [string](#string) |  | description of the task |
| start_time | [google.protobuf.Timestamp](#google-protobuf-Timestamp) |  | task must start by at least this time. Start time is combination of appointment date and time |
| estimate_time | [google.protobuf.Duration](#google-protobuf-Duration) |  | the estimated time period to complete the task |
| is_variation | [bool](#bool) |  | flag to confirm if the task is variation or not |
| is_vary | [bool](#bool) |  | flag to confirm if the task is vary or not |
| is_break | [bool](#bool) |  | update break to true or false |
| break_type | [string](#string) |  | update break to true or false |
| task_type | [string](#string) |  | type of task |

<a name="fm-TaskService"></a>

### TaskService
service to manage tasks

| Method Name | Request Type | Response Type | Description |
| ----------- | ------------ | ------------- | ------------|
| Create | [CreateTaskRequest](#fm-CreateTaskRequest) | [CreateTaskResponse](#fm-CreateTaskResponse) | Create a new task. Authorization scope of `fm.task.create` is required. |
| Checkin | [CheckinTaskRequest](#fm-CheckinTaskRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Checkin can be used to check in a staff to a task. Authorization scope of `fm.task.checkin` is required. |
| Checkout | [CheckoutTaskRequest](#fm-CheckoutTaskRequest) | [.google.protobuf.Empty](#google-protobuf-Empty) | Checkout can be used to check-out a staff from an existing checked-in task. Authorization scope of `fm.task.checkout` is required. |
| List | [ListTaskRequest](#fm-ListTaskRequest) | [ListTaskResponse](#fm-ListTaskResponse) | List returns the list of all tasks visible to the authorized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| ListTaskEmployee | [ListTaskEmployeeRequest](#fm-ListTaskEmployeeRequest) | [ListTaskEmployeeResponse](#fm-ListTaskEmployeeResponse) | Returns the list of employee ids of tasks visible to the authorized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| Detail | [TaskDetailRequest](#fm-TaskDetailRequest) | [TaskDetailResponse](#fm-TaskDetailResponse) | List returns the list of all tasks visible to the authorized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.task.detail` is required. |
| Update | [UpdateTaskRequest](#fm-UpdateTaskRequest) | [UpdateTaskResponse](#fm-UpdateTaskResponse) | Update an existing task. Authorization scope of `fm.task.update` is required. |
| UpdateRecurrence | [UpdateRecurrenceRequest](#fm-UpdateRecurrenceRequest) | [UpdateRecurrenceResponse](#fm-UpdateRecurrenceResponse) | Update task recurrence. Authorization scope of `fm.task.update` is required. |
| ListByClient | [ListTaskByClientRequest](#fm-ListTaskByClientRequest) | [ListTaskByClientResponse](#fm-ListTaskByClientResponse) | List returns the list of task by client visible to the authorized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.task.list-by-client` is required. |
| ListByEmployee | [ListTaskByEmployeeRequest](#fm-ListTaskByEmployeeRequest) | [ListTaskByEmployeeResponse](#fm-ListTaskByEmployeeResponse) | List returns the list of task by employee visible to the authorized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.task.list-by-employee` is required. |
| UpdateByEmployee | [UpdateTaskByEmployeeRequest](#fm-UpdateTaskByEmployeeRequest) | [UpdateTaskByEmployeeResponse](#fm-UpdateTaskByEmployeeResponse) | Update an existing task by employee_id Authorization scope of `fm.task.update-by-client` is required. |
| UpdateByClient | [UpdateTaskByClientRequest](#fm-UpdateTaskByClientRequest) | [UpdateTaskByClientResponse](#fm-UpdateTaskByClientResponse) | Update an existing task by client_id Authorization scope of `fm.task.update-by-client` is required. |
| ListByMobileEmployees | [ListTaskByMobileEmployeesRequest](#fm-ListTaskByMobileEmployeesRequest) | [ListTaskByMobileEmployeesResponse](#fm-ListTaskByMobileEmployeesResponse) | List returns the list of task by mobile employees visible to the authorized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.task.list-by-mobile-employees` is required. |
| ListByVariationClients | [ListTaskByVariationClientsRequest](#fm-ListTaskByVariationClientsRequest) | [ListTaskByVariationClientsResponse](#fm-ListTaskByVariationClientsResponse) | List returns the list of task by variation clients visible to the authorized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.task.list-by-variation-clients` is required. |
| ListPeriodic | [ListPeriodicTaskRequest](#fm-ListPeriodicTaskRequest) | [ListPeriodicTaskResponse](#fm-ListPeriodicTaskResponse) | List returns the list of periodic task clients visible to the authorized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.task.periodic` is required. |
| UpsertTaskCorrection | [UpsertTaskCorrectionRequest](#fm-UpsertTaskCorrectionRequest) | [UpsertTaskCorrectionResponse](#fm-UpsertTaskCorrectionResponse) | UpsertTaskCorrection creates or updates the task correction. Authorization scope of `fm.task.correction` is required. |
| ApproveTaskCorrection | [ApproveTaskCorrectionRequest](#fm-ApproveTaskCorrectionRequest) | [ApproveTaskCorrectionResponse](#fm-ApproveTaskCorrectionResponse) | ApproveTaskCorrection updates the status of task correction. Authorization scope of `fm.task.correction.approve` is required. |
| UpsertAllTaskCorrection | [UpsertAllTaskCorrectionRequest](#fm-UpsertAllTaskCorrectionRequest) | [UpsertAllTaskCorrectionResponse](#fm-UpsertAllTaskCorrectionResponse) | Creates new task-corrections or approves the existing ones. Authorization scope of `fm.task.correction.approve-all` is required. |
| ListCorrection | [ListCorrectionRequest](#fm-ListCorrectionRequest) | [ListCorrectionResponse](#fm-ListCorrectionResponse) | List returns the list of task corrections visible to the authorized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.task.correction.list` is required. |
| ChangeTimesheetCorrectionStatus | [ChangeTimesheetCorrectionStatusRequest](#fm-ChangeTimesheetCorrectionStatusRequest) | [ChangeTimesheetCorrectionStatusResponse](#fm-ChangeTimesheetCorrectionStatusResponse) | Change timesheet correction request status |
| ListTaskGroup | [TaskGroupRequest](#fm-TaskGroupRequest) | [TaskGroupResponse](#fm-TaskGroupResponse) | Task Group Data By Period (One of : Weekly, Monthly, Yearly) Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| ListAllTaskGroup | [AllTaskGroupRequest](#fm-AllTaskGroupRequest) | [AllTaskGroupResponse](#fm-AllTaskGroupResponse) | Task Group Data All Periods Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| ListTaskGroupByEmployee | [TaskGroupByEmployeeRequest](#fm-TaskGroupByEmployeeRequest) | [TaskGroupByEmployeeResponse](#fm-TaskGroupByEmployeeResponse) | Task Group Data By Employee Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| ListTaskGroupByClient | [TaskGroupByClientRequest](#fm-TaskGroupByClientRequest) | [TaskGroupByClientResponse](#fm-TaskGroupByClientResponse) | Task Group Data By Client Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| ListTaskGroupByAllClient | [ListTaskGroupByAllClientRequest](#fm-ListTaskGroupByAllClientRequest) | [ListTaskGroupByAllClientResponse](#fm-ListTaskGroupByAllClientResponse) | Task Group Data By all the Clients. Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| ListTaskGroupApproved | [TaskGroupRequest](#fm-TaskGroupRequest) | [TaskGroupResponse](#fm-TaskGroupResponse) | Task Group Data By Period (One of : Weekly, Monthly, Yearly) Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| ListAllTaskGroupApproved | [AllTaskGroupRequest](#fm-AllTaskGroupRequest) | [AllTaskGroupResponse](#fm-AllTaskGroupResponse) | Task Group Data All Periods Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| ListTaskGroupByEmployeeApproved | [TaskGroupByEmployeeRequest](#fm-TaskGroupByEmployeeRequest) | [TaskGroupByEmployeeResponse](#fm-TaskGroupByEmployeeResponse) | Task Group Data By Employee Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| ListTaskGroupByClientApproved | [TaskGroupByClientRequest](#fm-TaskGroupByClientRequest) | [TaskGroupByClientResponse](#fm-TaskGroupByClientResponse) | Task Group Data By Client Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| ListTaskGroupByAllClientApproved | [ListTaskGroupByAllClientRequest](#fm-ListTaskGroupByAllClientRequest) | [ListTaskGroupByAllClientResponse](#fm-ListTaskGroupByAllClientResponse) | Task Group Data By all the Clients. Authorization scope of `fm.task.list` is required. |
| UpdateTaskVarytime | [UpdateTaskVarytimeRequest](#fm-UpdateTaskVarytimeRequest) | [UpdateTaskVarytimeResponse](#fm-UpdateTaskVarytimeResponse) | Task Edit: Update Vary Time Authorization scope of `fm.task.update` is required. |
| CreateAbsence | [CreateAbsenceRequest](#fm-CreateAbsenceRequest) | [CreateAbsenceResponse](#fm-CreateAbsenceResponse) | Creates absence for an employee. Authorization scope of `fm.absence.create` is required. |
| ChangeAbsenceStatus | [ChangeAbsenceStatusRequest](#fm-ChangeAbsenceStatusRequest) | [ChangeAbsenceStatusResponse](#fm-ChangeAbsenceStatusResponse) | Change status of employee absence Authorization scope of `fm.absence.change-status` is required. |
| ListAbsence | [ListAbsenceRequest](#fm-ListAbsenceRequest) | [ListAbsenceResponse](#fm-ListAbsenceResponse) | ListAbsence returns the list of all employee absence visible to the authorized user in descending date order. Authorization scope of `fm.absence.list` is required. |
| UpdateAbsence | [UpdateAbsenceRequest](#fm-UpdateAbsenceRequest) | [UpdateAbsenceResponse](#fm-UpdateAbsenceResponse) | Updates the detail of an employee absence. Authorization scope of `fm.absence.update` is required. |
| CreateCover | [CreateCoverRequest](#fm-CreateCoverRequest) | [CreateCoverResponse](#fm-CreateCoverResponse) | Add Cover for absence Authorization scope of `fm.cover.create` is required. |

| .proto Type | Notes | C++ | Java | Python | Go | C# | PHP | Ruby |

| <a name="double" /> double |  | double | double | float | float64 | double | float | Float |
| <a name="float" /> float |  | float | float | float | float32 | float | float | Float |
| <a name="int32" /> int32 | Uses variable-length encoding. Inefficient for encoding negative numbers – if your field is likely to have negative values, use sint32 instead. | int32 | int | int | int32 | int | integer | Bignum or Fixnum (as required) |
| <a name="int64" /> int64 | Uses variable-length encoding. Inefficient for encoding negative numbers – if your field is likely to have negative values, use sint64 instead. | int64 | long | int/long | int64 | long | integer/string | Bignum |
| <a name="uint32" /> uint32 | Uses variable-length encoding. | uint32 | int | int/long | uint32 | uint | integer | Bignum or Fixnum (as required) |
| <a name="uint64" /> uint64 | Uses variable-length encoding. | uint64 | long | int/long | uint64 | ulong | integer/string | Bignum or Fixnum (as required) |
| <a name="sint32" /> sint32 | Uses variable-length encoding. Signed int value. These more efficiently encode negative numbers than regular int32s. | int32 | int | int | int32 | int | integer | Bignum or Fixnum (as required) |
| <a name="sint64" /> sint64 | Uses variable-length encoding. Signed int value. These more efficiently encode negative numbers than regular int64s. | int64 | long | int/long | int64 | long | integer/string | Bignum |
| <a name="fixed32" /> fixed32 | Always four bytes. More efficient than uint32 if values are often greater than 2^28. | uint32 | int | int | uint32 | uint | integer | Bignum or Fixnum (as required) |
| <a name="fixed64" /> fixed64 | Always eight bytes. More efficient than uint64 if values are often greater than 2^56. | uint64 | long | int/long | uint64 | ulong | integer/string | Bignum |
| <a name="sfixed32" /> sfixed32 | Always four bytes. | int32 | int | int | int32 | int | integer | Bignum or Fixnum (as required) |
| <a name="sfixed64" /> sfixed64 | Always eight bytes. | int64 | long | int/long | int64 | long | integer/string | Bignum |
| <a name="bool" /> bool |  | bool | boolean | boolean | bool | bool | boolean | TrueClass/FalseClass |
| <a name="string" /> string | A string must always contain UTF-8 encoded or 7-bit ASCII text. | string | String | str/unicode | string | string | string | String (UTF-8) |
| <a name="bytes" /> bytes | May contain any arbitrary sequence of bytes. | string | ByteString | str | []byte | ByteString | string | String (ASCII-8BIT) |
